## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: nonlinear oscillator dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models acceleration (dv/dt) in a nonlinear harmonic oscillator, where the restoring force depends nonlinearly on position x, and may include nonlinear damping in velocity v and/or time-dependent driving forces. The relationship dv/dt = F(x, v, t) follows Newton's second law.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Simple harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x (linear restoring force)
- Damped harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v (linear restoring + linear damping)
- Duffing oscillator (undriven): dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 (cubic nonlinear restoring force)
- Duffing oscillator (damped): dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v (cubic restoring + linear damping)
- Driven Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v + c3 * cos(c4 * t) (with periodic driving)
- Van der Pol oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * (1 - c2 * x**2) * v (nonlinear damping)
- Quintic nonlinearity: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x**5 (higher-order restoring force)
- Quadratic nonlinearity: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 (asymmetric restoring force)
- Nonlinear damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (cubic velocity damping)
- Coulomb + viscous damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v * abs(v) (quadratic drag)
- Mixed nonlinear: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x * v**2 (position-velocity coupling)
- Driven damped oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * sin(c3 * t) (sinusoidal driving force)
- Softening spring: dv_dt = c0 * x * (1 + c1 * x**2)**(-1) (rational restoring force)
- Pendulum-like: dv_dt = c0 * sin(c1 * x) (sinusoidal restoring force approximating pendulum)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope â†’ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects â†’ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay â†’ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior â†’ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects â†’ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Odd-power restoring forces (x, x^3, x^5) â†’ symmetric potential wells preserving oscillation symmetry
- Even-power position terms (x^2) â†’ asymmetric potential indicating broken reflection symmetry
- Velocity-dependent terms proportional to (1 - x^2)*v â†’ amplitude-dependent damping characteristic of self-sustained oscillators (Van der Pol type)
- Cubic position terms with sign opposite to linear term â†’ Duffing-type hardening or softening spring behavior
- Sinusoidal functions of time â†’ external periodic driving forces; frequency and phase encode resonance conditions
- Products of position powers and velocity powers (x^n * v^m) â†’ energy-dependent coupling between potential and kinetic contributions
- Sinusoidal functions of position â†’ pendulum-like dynamics where the small-angle approximation breaks down
- Odd functions of velocity in damping â†’ dissipation that respects time-reversal symmetry breaking consistently
